API Documentation

class Emoji

package texter.general

@:directlyUsed

The Emoji contains all of github's supported emojis.

In order to prevent lag, I didnt include the emojis as public fields, you can only get them from emojiFromString[] map or other methods

I want to thank PXshadow for making the emoji map, and making this class a possible thing

PXshadow's Github: https://github.com/PXshadow
